  <h1>Unapproved MAL Entries - Anime</h1>
  <div>
    This indexes approved and unapproved entries on MyAnimeList, displaying the currently unapproved queue. This feature isn't provided publicly on MAL itself. For some context:
  </div>
  <br />
  <div>
    Whenever an entry requested to be added (by a user), it gets an ID and is listed "on the website" - unlisted; at this point no one can add it to their list. If its approved it keeps that ID, else it becomes a 404. This acts as a index to check if you're submitting a duplicate, and to keep track of the current backlog. See the GitHub repo (top right) for more info.
  </div>
